<p>The <b>2014–15 Süper Lig</b> (known as the <i>Spor Toto Süper Lig</i> for sponsorship reasons) was the 57th season of the <a href="/wiki/S%C3%BCper_Lig" title="Süper Lig">Süper Lig</a>, the highest tier <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> league of <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Teams">Teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2014%E2%80%9315_S%C3%BCper_Lig&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><a href="/wiki/Elaz%C4%B1%C4%9Fspor" title="Elazığspor">Elazığspor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Antalyaspor" title="Antalyaspor">Antalyaspor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kayserispor" title="Kayserispor">Kayserispor</a> were relegated at the end of the 2013–14 season after finishing in the bottom three places of the standings. Elazığspor was at top level for 2 years, Antalyaspor and Kayserispor returned to second level after 6 and 10 years respectively. The relegated teams were replaced by 2013–14 TFF First League champions <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0stanbul_Ba%C5%9Fak%C5%9Fehir_F.K." title="İstanbul Başakşehir F.K.">İstanbul Başakşehir</a>, runners-up <a href="/wiki/Bal%C4%B1kesirspor" title="Balıkesirspor">Balıkesirspor</a> and play-off winners <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mersin_%C4%B0dmanyurdu_SK" title="Mersin İdmanyurdu SK">Mersin İdmanyurdu</a>. They returned to the top division after 1, 38 and 1 years respectively.</p>

<li id="cite_note-table_note_BUR0.69403132036982-38"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-table_note_BUR0.69403132036982_38-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Bursaspor" title="Bursaspor">Bursaspor</a>, finalist of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Turkish_Cup" title="2014–15 Turkish Cup">2014–15 Turkish Cup</a>, was banned by UEFA from competing in the 2015–16 UEFA Europa League even if they qualify.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37"><a href="#cite_note-37">[36]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982-40"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982_40-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982_40-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982_40-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982_40-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982_40-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_note_M.C4.B0Y0.69403132036982_40-5"><sup><i><b>f</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Mersin İdmanyurdu, Gaziantepspor, Eskişehirspor, Balıkesirspor, Kasımpaşa and Kayseri Erciyesspor could not get an UEFA licence. Therefore, even if they get right to play in Europe due to their final standing, they will lose their right.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[37]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-table_hth_GEN0.69403132036982-41"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-table_hth_GEN0.69403132036982_41-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_hth_GEN0.69403132036982_41-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Gençlerbirliği ahead on head-to-head record; Gençlerbirliği–Gaziantepspor 2–0, Gaziantepspor–Gençlerbirliği 0–3.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-table_hth_.C3.87AY0.69403132036982-42"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-table_hth_.C3.87AY0.69403132036982_42-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_hth_.C3.87AY0.69403132036982_42-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Çaykur Rizespor ahead on head-to-head record; Çaykur Rizespor–Sivasspor 2–1, Sivasspor–Çaykur Rizespor 0–1.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-table_hth_KEC0.69403132036982-43"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-table_hth_KEC0.69403132036982_43-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-table_hth_KEC0.69403132036982_43-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Kayseri Erciyesspor ahead on head-to-head record; Kayseri Erciyesspor–Balıkesirspor 4–0, Balıkesirspor–Kayseri Erciyesspor 1–1.</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
